\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{Pixel\+Format}{PixelFormat}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}\#define Pixel\+Format~{\bf A\+V\+Pixel\+Format}}\hypertarget{pixfmt_8h_a4cd89786474394431e3c9cfe5ae86708}{}\label{pixfmt_8h_a4cd89786474394431e3c9cfe5ae86708}


Definition at line 354 of file pixfmt.\+h.



\subsection{Enumeration Type Documentation}
\index{pixfmt.\+h@{pixfmt.\+h}!A\+V\+Pixel\+Format@{A\+V\+Pixel\+Format}}
\index{A\+V\+Pixel\+Format@{A\+V\+Pixel\+Format}!pixfmt.\+h@{pixfmt.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{A\+V\+Pixel\+Format}{AVPixelFormat}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}enum {\bf A\+V\+Pixel\+Format}}\hypertarget{pixfmt_8h_a9a8e335cf3be472042bc9f0cf80cd4c5}{}\label{pixfmt_8h_a9a8e335cf3be472042bc9f0cf80cd4c5}
Pixel format.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
A\+V\+\_\+\+P\+I\+X\+\_\+\+F\+M\+T\+\_\+\+R\+G\+B32 is handled in an endian-\/specific manner. An R\+G\+BA color is put together as\+: (A $<$$<$ 24) $\vert$ (R $<$$<$ 16) $\vert$ (G $<$$<$ 8) $\vert$ B This is stored as B\+G\+RA on little-\/endian C\+PU architectures and A\+R\+GB on big-\/endian C\+P\+Us.
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
When the pixel format is palettized R\+GB (A\+V\+\_\+\+P\+I\+X\+\_\+\+F\+M\+T\+\_\+\+P\+A\+L8), the palettized image data is stored in \hyperlink{struct_a_v_frame_a1d0f65014a8d1bf78cec8cbed2304992}{A\+V\+Frame.\+data}\mbox{[}0\mbox{]}. The palette is transported in \hyperlink{struct_a_v_frame_a1d0f65014a8d1bf78cec8cbed2304992}{A\+V\+Frame.\+data}\mbox{[}1\mbox{]}, is 1024 bytes long (256 4-\/byte entries) and is formatted the same as in A\+V\+\_\+\+P\+I\+X\+\_\+\+F\+M\+T\+\_\+\+R\+G\+B32 described above (i.\+e., it is also endian-\/specific). Note also that the individual R\+GB palette components stored in \hyperlink{struct_a_v_frame_a1d0f65014a8d1bf78cec8cbed2304992}{A\+V\+Frame.\+data}\mbox{[}1\mbox{]} should be in the range 0..255. This is important as many custom P\+A\+L8 video codecs that were designed to run on the I\+BM V\+GA graphics adapter use 6-\/bit palette components.
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{}
For all the 8bit per pixel formats, an R\+G\+B32 palette is in data\mbox{[}1\mbox{]} like for pal8. This palette is filled in automatically by the function allocating the picture.
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Make sure that all newly added big-\/endian formats have (pix\+\_\+fmt \& 1) == 1 and that all newly added little-\/endian formats have (pix\+\_\+fmt \& 1) == 0. This allows simpler detection of big vs little-\/endian. 
\end{DoxyNote}
